The remaining mismatch is likely isolated to the MFMA tile layout, so I’m switching to a tiny one-tile diagnostic kernel. That lets me validate the lane-to-matrix mapping directly without rerunning the full benchmark model.

import torch, substrate, substrate.language as S

@substrate.jit
def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((64,16), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((16,64), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((64,64), S.f32)):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % 64
    wave = tid // 64
    wave_m = wave // 2
    wave_n = wave % 2
    lane_row = lane % 32
    lane_half = lane // 32
    row = wave_m * 32 + lane_row
    a_shared = S.make_shared((256,4), S.u32)
    b_shared = S.make_shared((256,4), S.u32)
    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    # A/B packing copied from output kernel for one K_TILE=16 and one 64x64 macro-tile.
    a_load_k = lane_half * 8
    a_view = S.view(A[row, a_load_k], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
    a_wave_base = wave * 64
    if lane_half == 0:
        a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_view[0]
        a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_view[1]
        a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_view[2]
        a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_view[3]
    else:
        a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_view[0]
        a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_view[1]
        a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_view[2]
        a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_view[3]

    b_local = lane % 32
    b_col_pack = b_local % 2
    b_k_pack = b_local // 2
    b_col = wave_n * 32 + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
    b_row = b_k_pack
    b_view = S.view(B[b_row, b_col], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
    b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
    if b_k_pack < 8:
        b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
        b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_view[0]
        b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_view[1]
        b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_view[2]
        b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_view[3]
    else:
        b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
        b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_view[0]
        b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_view[1]
        b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_view[2]
        b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_view[3]

    S.syncthreads()
    a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2,4,1), S.bf16))
    b_frag = S.view(b_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2,4,1), S.bf16))
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

    col_base = wave_n * 32 + lane_half * 16
    for i in S.range(16):
        C[row, col_base + i] = acc[i]

def launch():
    return ((1,1,1),(256,1,1))

torch.manual_seed(0)
A = torch.randn((64,16), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
B = torch.randn((16,64), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
C = torch.zeros((64,64), device='cuda', dtype=torch.float32)

# compile + run
try:
    test_kernel[launch](A,B,C)
    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
    diff = (C - ref).abs()
    print('max', diff.max().item(), 'mean', diff.mean().item())
    print('row0', C[0,:16].cpu().tolist())
    print('ref0', ref[0,:16].cpu().tolist())
except Exception as e:
    print('ERR', type(e).__name__, e)

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = lane % 32
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_frag = S.view(b_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        col_base = wave_col + lane_half * 16
+        bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 0], S.f32)
+        bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 1], S.f32)
+        bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 2], S.f32)
+        bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 3], S.f32)
+        bias4 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 4], S.f32)
+        bias5 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 5], S.f32)
+        bias6 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 6], S.f32)
+        bias7 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 7], S.f32)
+        bias8 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 8], S.f32)
+        bias9 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 9], S.f32)
+        bias10 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 10], S.f32)
+        bias11 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 11], S.f32)
+        bias12 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 12], S.f32)
+        bias13 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 13], S.f32)
+        bias14 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 14], S.f32)
+        bias15 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 15], S.f32)
+        Y[row, col_base + 0] = S.convert(acc[0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 1] = S.convert(acc[1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 2] = S.convert(acc[2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 3] = S.convert(acc[3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 4] = S.convert(acc[4] + bias4, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 5] = S.convert(acc[5] + bias5, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 6] = S.convert(acc[6] + bias6, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 7] = S.convert(acc[7] + bias7, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 8] = S.convert(acc[8] + bias8, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 9] = S.convert(acc[9] + bias9, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 10] = S.convert(acc[10] + bias10, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 11] = S.convert(acc[11] + bias11, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 12] = S.convert(acc[12] + bias12, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 13] = S.convert(acc[13] + bias13, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 14] = S.convert(acc[14] + bias14, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 15] = S.convert(acc[15] + bias15, S.bf16)
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for rg_tile in S.range((BLOCK_M * NUM_GROUPS) // THREADS_PER_BLOCK):
+        rg = rg_tile * THREADS_PER_BLOCK + tid
+        rg_row = block_row + (rg // NUM_GROUPS)
+        g = rg % NUM_GROUPS
+        base = g * GROUP_SIZE
+
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
 
-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
 
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = base + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[rg_row, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            if v < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+            if v > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+            Y[rg_row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
         super().__init__()
         self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
         self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
         self.hardtanh = nn.Hardtanh(min_val=hardtanh_min, max_val=hardtanh_max)
+        self._cache_key = None
+        self._cached_w_t = None
 
+    def _prepare_params(self, x):
+        weight = self.gemm.weight
+        bias = self.gemm.bias
+        gn_w = self.group_norm.weight
+        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias
+        device = x.device
+        dtype = x.dtype
+        key = (
+            device,
+            dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            gn_w.data_ptr(),
+            gn_b.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_w_t = weight.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+
+        if bias.device == device and bias.dtype == dtype:
+            bias_arg = bias
+        else:
+            bias_arg = bias.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_w.device == device and gn_w.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w
+        else:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_b.device == device and gn_b.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b
+        else:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        return self._cached_w_t, bias_arg, gn_w_arg, gn_b_arg

+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
         super().__init__()
         self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
         self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)

+    def _prepare_params(self, x):
+        weight = self.gemm.weight
+        bias = self.gemm.bias
+        gn_w = self.group_norm.weight
+        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias
+        device = x.device
+        dtype = x.dtype
+        key = (
+            device,
+            dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            gn_w.data_ptr(),
+            gn_b.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_w_t = weight.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+
+        if bias.device == device and bias.dtype == dtype:
+            bias_arg = bias
+        else:
+            bias_arg = bias.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_w.device == device and gn_w.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w
+        else:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_b.device == device and gn_b.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b
+        else:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        return self._cached_w_t, bias_arg, gn_w_arg, gn_b_arg

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()

+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

+            S.syncthreads()

+        bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 0], S.f32)

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_frag = S.view(b_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        col_base = wave_col + lane_half * 16
+        bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 0], S.f32)
+        bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 1], S.f32)
+        bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 2], S.f32)
+        bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 3], S.f32)
+        bias4 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 4], S.f32)
+        bias5 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 5], S.f32)
+        bias6 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 6], S.f32)
+        bias7 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 7], S.f32)
+        bias8 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 8], S.f32)
+        bias9 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 9], S.f32)
+        bias10 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 10], S.f32)
+        bias11 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 11], S.f32)
+        bias12 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 12], S.f32)
+        bias13 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 13], S.f32)
+        bias14 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 14], S.f32)
+        bias15 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 15], S.f32)
+        Y[row, col_base + 0] = S.convert(acc[0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 1] = S.convert(acc[1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 2] = S.convert(acc[2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 3] = S.convert(acc[3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 4] = S.convert(acc[4] + bias4, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 5] = S.convert(acc[5] + bias5, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 6] = S.convert(acc[6] + bias6, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 7] = S.convert(acc[7] + bias7, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 8] = S.convert(acc[8] + bias8, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 9] = S.convert(acc[9] + bias9, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 10] = S.convert(acc[10] + bias10, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 11] = S.convert(acc[11] + bias11, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 12] = S.convert(acc[12] + bias12, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 13] = S.convert(acc[13] + bias13, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 14] = S.convert(acc[14] + bias14, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 15] = S.convert(acc[15] + bias15, S.bf16)
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for rg_tile in S.range((BLOCK_M * NUM_GROUPS) // THREADS_PER_BLOCK):
+        rg = rg_tile * THREADS_PER_BLOCK + tid
+        rg_row = block_row + (rg // NUM_GROUPS)
+        g = rg % NUM_GROUPS
+        base = g * GROUP_SIZE
+
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)

+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))

+            if v > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+            Y[rg_row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
         super().__init__()
         self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
         self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
         self.hardtanh = nn.Hardtanh(min_val=hardtanh_min, max_val=hardtanh_max)
+        self._cache_key = None
+        self._cached_w_t = None
 
+    def _prepare_params(self, x):
+        weight = self.gemm.weight
+        bias = self.gemm.bias
+        gn_w = self.group_norm.weight
+        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias
+        device = x.device
+        dtype = x.dtype
+        key = (
+            device,
+            dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            gn_w.data_ptr(),
+            gn_b.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_w_t = weight.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+
+        if bias.device == device and bias.dtype == dtype:
+            bias_arg = bias
+        else:
+            bias_arg = bias.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_w.device == device and gn_w.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w
+        else:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_b.device == device and gn_b.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b
+        else:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        return self._cached_w_t, bias_arg, gn_w_arg, gn_b_arg

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2

+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16

+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M

I’m checking a zero-input case next. That isolates whether the post-GEMM normalization path is correct and whether the MFMA path collapses cleanly to just the bias term, without needing the slow naive reference kernel.

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:

+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

+            S.syncthreads()

+        col_base = wave_col + lane_half * 16

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_frag = S.view(b_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        col_base = wave_col + lane_half * 16
+        bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 0], S.f32)
+        bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 1], S.f32)
+        bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 2], S.f32)
+        bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 3], S.f32)
+        bias4 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 4], S.f32)
+        bias5 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 5], S.f32)
+        bias6 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 6], S.f32)
+        bias7 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 7], S.f32)
+        bias8 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 8], S.f32)
+        bias9 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 9], S.f32)
+        bias10 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 10], S.f32)
+        bias11 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 11], S.f32)
+        bias12 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 12], S.f32)
+        bias13 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 13], S.f32)
+        bias14 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 14], S.f32)
+        bias15 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 15], S.f32)
+        Y[row, col_base + 0] = S.convert(acc[0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 1] = S.convert(acc[1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 2] = S.convert(acc[2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 3] = S.convert(acc[3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 4] = S.convert(acc[4] + bias4, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 5] = S.convert(acc[5] + bias5, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 6] = S.convert(acc[6] + bias6, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 7] = S.convert(acc[7] + bias7, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 8] = S.convert(acc[8] + bias8, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 9] = S.convert(acc[9] + bias9, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 10] = S.convert(acc[10] + bias10, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 11] = S.convert(acc[11] + bias11, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 12] = S.convert(acc[12] + bias12, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 13] = S.convert(acc[13] + bias13, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 14] = S.convert(acc[14] + bias14, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 15] = S.convert(acc[15] + bias15, S.bf16)

+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for rg_tile in S.range((BLOCK_M * NUM_GROUPS) // THREADS_PER_BLOCK):

+        g = rg % NUM_GROUPS

+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):

+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
         super().__init__()
         self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
         self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
         self.hardtanh = nn.Hardtanh(min_val=hardtanh_min, max_val=hardtanh_max)
+        self._cache_key = None
+        self._cached_w_t = None
 
+    def _prepare_params(self, x):
+        weight = self.gemm.weight
+        bias = self.gemm.bias
+        gn_w = self.group_norm.weight
+        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias
+        device = x.device
+        dtype = x.dtype
+        key = (
+            device,
+            dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            gn_w.data_ptr(),
+            gn_b.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_w_t = weight.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+
+        if bias.device == device and bias.dtype == dtype:
+            bias_arg = bias
+        else:
+            bias_arg = bias.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_w.device == device and gn_w.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w
+        else:

+

+            gn_b_arg = gn_b
+        else:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)

I’ve confirmed the normalization path is exact on zero input, so I’m isolating the GEMM layout by making GroupNorm affine an identity in a debug run. That turns the remaining error into a direct permutation/signature problem on the GEMM output tiles.

/bin/bash -lc "/opt/venv/bin/python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, torch
out='/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p30/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py'
spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('opt',out)
m=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
spec.loader.exec_module(m)
model=m.ModelNew(m.IN_FEATURES,m.OUT_FEATURES,m.NUM_GROUPS,m.HARDTANH_MIN,m.HARDTANH_MAX).cuda().bfloat16().eval()
with torch.no_grad():
    model.group_norm.weight.fill_(1)
    model.group_norm.bias.zero_()
    x=torch.zeros((m.BATCH_SIZE,m.IN_FEATURES),device='cuda',dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    x[0,0]=1
    y=model(x)[0].float().cpu()
    lin=(x[0].float() @ model._prepare_params(x)[0].float()) + model.gemm.bias.float()
    ref=torch.nn.functional.group_norm(lin.view(1,-1), m.NUM_GROUPS, model.group_norm.weight.float(), model.group_norm.bias.float(), m.EPS)
    ref=torch.clamp(ref, m.HARDTANH_MIN, m.HARDTANH_MAX)[0].cpu()
    d=(y-ref).abs()
    print('max', d.max().item(), 'mean', d.mean().item())
    print('y0', y[:32].tolist())
    print('r0', ref[:32].tolist())
    # For the first 32 values, print nearest ref index within same 32 tile.
    for base in [0,32,64,96]:
        tile_y=y[base:base+32]
        tile_r=ref[base:base+32]
        idx=[]
        used=set()
        for v in tile_y.tolist():
            best=None
            bestj=None
            for j,u in enumerate(tile_r.tolist()):
                if j in used:
                    continue
                dv=abs(v-u)
                if best is None or dv<best:
                    best=dv; bestj=j
            used.add(bestj)
            idx.append(bestj)
        print('tile',base,'perm',idx)

+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
         super().__init__()
         self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)

+    def _prepare_params(self, x):
+        weight = self.gemm.weight
+        bias = self.gemm.bias
+        gn_w = self.group_norm.weight
+        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias
+        device = x.device
+        dtype = x.dtype
+        key = (
+            device,
+            dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            gn_w.data_ptr(),
+            gn_b.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_w_t = weight.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+
+        if bias.device == device and bias.dtype == dtype:

+
+        if gn_w.device == device and gn_w.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w

+

+            gn_b_arg = gn_b
+        else:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        return self._cached_w_t, bias_arg, gn_w_arg, gn_b_arg

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+

+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row

+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)

+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):

+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N

+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8

+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)

+            a_wave_base = wave * 64

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_frag = S.view(b_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        col_base = wave_col + lane_half * 16
+        bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 0], S.f32)
+        bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 1], S.f32)
+        bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 2], S.f32)
+        bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 3], S.f32)
+        bias4 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 4], S.f32)
+        bias5 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 5], S.f32)
+        bias6 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 6], S.f32)
+        bias7 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 7], S.f32)
+        bias8 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 8], S.f32)
+        bias9 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 9], S.f32)
+        bias10 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 10], S.f32)
+        bias11 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 11], S.f32)
+        bias12 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 12], S.f32)
+        bias13 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 13], S.f32)
+        bias14 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 14], S.f32)
+        bias15 = S.convert(BIAS0[col_base + 15], S.f32)
+        Y[row, col_base + 0] = S.convert(acc[0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 1] = S.convert(acc[1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 2] = S.convert(acc[2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 3] = S.convert(acc[3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 4] = S.convert(acc[4] + bias4, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 5] = S.convert(acc[5] + bias5, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 6] = S.convert(acc[6] + bias6, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 7] = S.convert(acc[7] + bias7, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 8] = S.convert(acc[8] + bias8, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 9] = S.convert(acc[9] + bias9, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 10] = S.convert(acc[10] + bias10, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 11] = S.convert(acc[11] + bias11, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 12] = S.convert(acc[12] + bias12, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 13] = S.convert(acc[13] + bias13, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 14] = S.convert(acc[14] + bias14, S.bf16)
+        Y[row, col_base + 15] = S.convert(acc[15] + bias15, S.bf16)
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for rg_tile in S.range((BLOCK_M * NUM_GROUPS) // THREADS_PER_BLOCK):
+        rg = rg_tile * THREADS_PER_BLOCK + tid
+        rg_row = block_row + (rg // NUM_GROUPS)
+        g = rg % NUM_GROUPS
+        base = g * GROUP_SIZE
+
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
 
-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
 
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = base + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[rg_row, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            if v < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+            if v > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+            Y[rg_row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
         super().__init__()
         self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
         self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
         self.hardtanh = nn.Hardtanh(min_val=hardtanh_min, max_val=hardtanh_max)
+        self._cache_key = None
+        self._cached_w_t = None
 
+    def _prepare_params(self, x):
+        weight = self.gemm.weight
+        bias = self.gemm.bias
+        gn_w = self.group_norm.weight
+        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias
+        device = x.device
+        dtype = x.dtype
+        key = (
+            device,
+            dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            gn_w.data_ptr(),
+            gn_b.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_w_t = weight.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+
+        if bias.device == device and bias.dtype == dtype:
+            bias_arg = bias
+        else:
+            bias_arg = bias.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_w.device == device and gn_w.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w
+        else:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_b.device == device and gn_b.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b
+        else:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        return self._cached_w_t, bias_arg, gn_w_arg, gn_b_arg
+

+        device = x.device
+        dtype = x.dtype
+        key = (

+            dtype,

+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            gn_w.data_ptr(),
+            gn_b.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_w_t = weight.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:

+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]

I’ve isolated the problem to the MFMA accumulator scatter. I’m trying the most plausible alternative accumulator layout next: a `4 x 4` fragment per lane written through the tile, while leaving the operand staging unchanged.

 HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_M = 32

+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_TILE = 16

-def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_frag = S.view(b_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        row_base = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + (lane % 8)
+        col_base = wave_col + (lane // 8) * 4
+        for rr in S.range(4):
+            out_row = row_base + rr * 8
+            acc_base = rr * 4
+            for cc in S.range(4):
+                out_col = col_base + cc
+                Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(
+                    acc[acc_base + cc] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32),
+                    S.bf16,
+                )
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for rg_tile in S.range((BLOCK_M * NUM_GROUPS) // THREADS_PER_BLOCK):
+        rg = rg_tile * THREADS_PER_BLOCK + tid
+        rg_row = block_row + (rg // NUM_GROUPS)
+        g = rg % NUM_GROUPS
+        base = g * GROUP_SIZE
+
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = base + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[rg_row, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            if v < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+            if v > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+            Y[rg_row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
         super().__init__()
         self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
         self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
         self.hardtanh = nn.Hardtanh(min_val=hardtanh_min, max_val=hardtanh_max)
+        self._cache_key = None
+        self._cached_w_t = None
+
+    def _prepare_params(self, x):
+        weight = self.gemm.weight
+        bias = self.gemm.bias
+        gn_w = self.group_norm.weight
+        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias
+        device = x.device
+        dtype = x.dtype
+        key = (
+            device,
+            dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            gn_w.data_ptr(),
+            gn_b.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_w_t = weight.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+
+        if bias.device == device and bias.dtype == dtype:
+            bias_arg = bias
+        else:
+            bias_arg = bias.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_w.device == device and gn_w.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w
+        else:
+            gn_w_arg = gn_w.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        if gn_b.device == device and gn_b.dtype == dtype:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b
+        else:
+            gn_b_arg = gn_b.to(device=device, dtype=dtype)
+
+        return self._cached_w_t, bias_arg, gn_w_arg, gn_b_arg

+        base = g * GROUP_SIZE
+
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = base + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[rg_row, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            if v < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+            if v > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+            Y[rg_row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_frag = S.view(b_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        row_base = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + (lane % 8)
+        col_base = wave_col + (lane // 8) * 4
+        for rr in S.range(4):
+            out_row = row_base + rr * 8
+            acc_base = rr * 4
+            for cc in S.range(4):
+                out_col = col_base + cc
+                Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(
+                    acc[acc_base + cc] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32),
+                    S.bf16,
+                )
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for rg_tile in S.range((BLOCK_M * NUM_GROUPS) // THREADS_PER_BLOCK):
+        rg = rg_tile * THREADS_PER_BLOCK + tid
+        rg_row = block_row + (rg // NUM_GROUPS)
+        g = rg % NUM_GROUPS
+        base = g * GROUP_SIZE
+
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = base + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[rg_row, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            if v < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+            if v > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+            Y[rg_row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_frag = S.view(b_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        row_base = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + (lane % 8)
+        col_base = wave_col + (lane // 8) * 4
+        for rr in S.range(4):
+            out_row = row_base + rr * 8
+            acc_base = rr * 4
+            for cc in S.range(4):
+                out_col = col_base + cc
+                Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(
+                    acc[acc_base + cc] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32),
+                    S.bf16,
+                )
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for rg_tile in S.range((BLOCK_M * NUM_GROUPS) // THREADS_PER_BLOCK):
+        rg = rg_tile * THREADS_PER_BLOCK + tid
+        rg_row = block_row + (rg // NUM_GROUPS)
+        g = rg % NUM_GROUPS
+        base = g * GROUP_SIZE
+
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = base + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[rg_row, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            if v < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+            if v > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+            Y[rg_row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

         fused_kernel[_launch](x.contiguous(), w_t, bias, gn_w, gn_b, y)
         return y

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    wave = tid // 64
+    wave_m = wave // 2
+    wave_n = wave % 2
+    lane_row = (lane % 16) + ((lane // 16) % 2) * 16
+    lane_half = lane // 32
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    row = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + lane_row
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_frag = S.view(b_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        row_base = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + (lane % 8)
+        col_base = wave_col + (lane // 8) * 4
+        for rr in S.range(4):
+            out_row = row_base + rr * 8
+            acc_base = rr * 4
+            for cc in S.range(4):
+                out_col = col_base + cc
+                Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(
+                    acc[acc_base + cc] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32),
+                    S.bf16,
+                )
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for rg_tile in S.range((BLOCK_M * NUM_GROUPS) // THREADS_PER_BLOCK):
+        rg = rg_tile * THREADS_PER_BLOCK + tid
+        rg_row = block_row + (rg // NUM_GROUPS)
+        g = rg % NUM_GROUPS
+        base = g * GROUP_SIZE
+
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = base + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[rg_row, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            if v < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+            if v > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+            Y[rg_row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+    a_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    for n_tile in S.range(OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N):
+        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        wave_col = n_tile * BLOCK_N + wave_n * WAVE_N
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE):
+            k_base = k_tile * K_TILE
+            a_load_k = k_base + lane_half * 8
+            a_byte_offset = S.convert(((row * IN_FEATURES) + a_load_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            a_wave_base = wave * 64
+            if lane_half == 0:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 0] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 1] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 0] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 1] = a_words[3]
+            else:
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 2] = a_words[0]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row, 3] = a_words[1]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 2] = a_words[2]
+                a_shared[a_wave_base + lane_row + 32, 3] = a_words[3]
+
+            b_local = lane % 32
+            b_col_pack = b_local % 2
+            b_k_pack = b_local // 2
+            b_col = wave_col + lane_half * 16 + b_col_pack * 8
+            b_row = k_base + b_k_pack
+            b_byte_offset = S.convert(((b_row * OUT_FEATURES) + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+            b_wave_base = wave * 64 + lane_half * 32
+            if b_k_pack < 8:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + b_k_pack * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 0] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 1] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 0] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 1] = b_words[3]
+            else:
+                b_slot = b_wave_base + (b_k_pack - 8) * 4 + b_col_pack * 2
+                b_shared[b_slot, 2] = b_words[0]
+                b_shared[b_slot, 3] = b_words[1]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 2] = b_words[2]
+                b_shared[b_slot + 1, 3] = b_words[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_frag = S.view(b_shared[wave * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        row_base = block_row + wave_m * WAVE_M + (lane % 8)
+        col_base = wave_col + (lane // 8) * 4
+        for rr in S.range(4):
+            out_row = row_base + rr * 8
+            acc_base = rr * 4
+            for cc in S.range(4):
+                out_col = col_base + cc
+                Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(
+                    acc[acc_base + cc] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32),
+                    S.bf16,
+                )
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for rg_tile in S.range((BLOCK_M * NUM_GROUPS) // THREADS_PER_BLOCK):
+        rg = rg_tile * THREADS_PER_BLOCK + tid
+        rg_row = block_row + (rg // NUM_GROUPS)
+        g = rg % NUM_GROUPS
+        base = g * GROUP_SIZE
+
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[rg_row, base + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = base + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[rg_row, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            if v < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+            if v > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+                v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+            Y[rg_row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

I’m making one last focused accumulator-scatter adjustment by swapping the `4 x 4` lane grid axes. If that doesn’t materially improve the one-row perturbation behavior, I’ll stop rather than churn on arbitrary mappings.

+    tid = S.thread_id(0)

+K_TILE = 16
+
+
+def _launch():
+    return ((1, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
